_ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="">INTRODUCTION</h2><ol _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166=""><li _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="">Eyeora Ltd, a company registered in England under company number 10825902 and whose registered office is 7 Bell Yard, London, England, WC2A 2JR, and its affiliate companies (“EYEORA”, “we”, “us” or “our” in this policy), operates the Eyeora platforms (including the virtual reality technologies, applications, products, software and other materials under the “EYEORA” brand) (“Services”). This policy explains how we will process the personal data relating to users of the Services. <p _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="" class="mt-3">"If you have any questions or comments about this policy please contact us <a _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="" href="https://www.eyeora-vr.com/contact-us" target="_blank" class="txt_btn txt_btn_updated d-inline-flex fs14 lh1"><span _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="">here</span></a> (please categorise your message as “Privacy”)"</p></li><li _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="">EYEORA is committed to protecting and respecting your privacy. This policy explains the basis on which personal data we collect from you will be processed by us. Where we decide the purpose or means for which Personal Data you supply through these Services is processed, we are the “data controller” for the purposes of the General Data Protection Regulation 2016/679 (as may be amended or replaced by equivalent legislation in the UK from time to time).</li><li _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166=""><p _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="">This policy explains the following:</p><ol _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166=""><li _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="">What information EYEORA may collect about you;</li><li _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="">How EYEORA will use information we collect about you;</li><li _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="">Whether EYEORA will disclose your details to anyone else;</li><li _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="">Your choices and rights regarding the personal data you have provided to us; and</li><li _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="">The main cookies we use and why.</li></ol></li><li _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="">Our online services contain hyperlinks to websites owned and operated by third parties. These third-party websites may have their own privacy policies and we recommend that you review them. We do not accept any responsibility or liability for the privacy practices of such third parties and your use of their services is at your own risk.</li></ol></li><li _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166=""><h2 _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="">WHAT INFORMATION WILL EYEORA COLLECT ABOUT ME?</h2><ol _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166=""><li _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="">We collect and process the following information which may include your Personal Data.</li><h4 _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="" class="text-lg-center mt-4 mb-3">Information provided by you when using our Services</h4><p _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="">You may give us information about you by filling in forms when setting up an account with us, using our Services, signing up to our newsletter or contacting us with enquiries. Such information may include:</p><p _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="">1) Identity and log-in data: including your name, username, virtual avatar, profession, profile picture, e-mail address and password;</p><p _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="">2) Transaction data: where you host, upload, attend, or access paid virtual content or event, purchase a subscription or access other paid-for items, we will keep information related to your purchases and transactions relating to you (see the section on Payment Information below);</p><p _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="">3) XR rooms/Event data: this is information related to the XR rooms and events that you host or attend, including any content, audio and visual recordings of those events, actions that you take and copies of chat logs and interactions between you and other users;</p><p _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="">4) Your enquiry: if you contact us about your account and/or our Services, we may keep the content of such enquiry. You are under no obligation to provide us with any details, but if you do not provide all relevant information, we may not be able to help.</p><h4 _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="" class="text-lg-center mt-4 mb-3">Payment Information</h4><p _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="">When you pay for access to virtual events or other Services, we use the third party payment system provided by Stripe &amp; 2Checkout, which transacts all our payments. Where you make a payment, 2Checkout and Stripe will collect your name, credit card, billing address, delivery address (if applicable) and email address for payment processing. Card payment information is collected by 2Checkout and Stripe directly through their APIs which means that Eyeora has no access to your card payment information. For further details of how 2Checkout collects and uses personal data please see their privacy policy <a _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="" href="https://www.2checkout.com/legal/privacy/" class="txt_btn txt_btn_updated d-inline-flex fs14 lh1"><span _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="">here</span></a> and for Stripe please <a _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="" href="https://stripe.com/privacy" class="txt_btn txt_btn_updated d-inline-flex fs14 lh1"><span _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="">click here</span></a>.</p><h4 _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="" class="text-lg-center mt-4 mb-3">How you use the Services (Analytics)</h4><p _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="" class="d-block">When you use the Services, we collect the following information:</p><p _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="" class="d-block">1) How often you use our Services and how you use our Services;</p><p _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="" class="d-block">2) Your IP address; and</p><p _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="" class="d-block">3) Device and browser operating system, version, make and model.</p><p _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="" class="d-block">Please see Part 2 of this Privacy and Cookie Policy for further details.</p></ol></li><li _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166=""><h2 _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="">DATA SHARING</h2><ol _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166=""><li _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166=""> As reasonably necessary for the purposes set out in this privacy policy, we may share your personal information with carefully-selected third parties (including suppliers and subcontractors), who are engaged to help us run, market, manage and improve the quality of the services that we offer. Where such investigation concludes in a ban from our Services, we will keep details of such ban to ensure that it can be enforced.</p><p _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="">We process information for the legitimate interest of complying with HMRC requirements by retaining records of customer purchases and transactions.</p><p _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="">Where we reasonably believe that you are or may be in breach of any of the applicable laws or regulations, we may use your personal data to inform relevant third parties, your email/internet provider or law enforcement agencies about the content.</p></li><li _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166=""><h2 _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="" class="d-inline">YOUR RIGHTS IN RELATION TO PERSONAL DATA WHICH WE PROCESS RELATING TO YOU</h2><ol _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="" class="mt-3"><li _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166=""><p _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="">You have the following rights over the way we process personal data relating to you. This information is held by us indefinitely, consistent with our legitimate interest and reviewed periodically.</li><li _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="">In some circumstances we may anonymise your personal data (so that it can no longer be associated with you) for research or statistical purposes in which case we may use this information indefinitely without further notice to you.</li></ol></li><li _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166=""><h2 _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="">CHILDREN</h2><p _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="">We do not knowingly solicit data from or market to children under the age of 13. We will delete such information from our files within a reasonable time. </p></li><li _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166=""><h2 _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="">SECURITY</h2><ol _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166=""><li _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="">We will take all reasonable technical and organisational precautions to prevent the loss, misuse or alteration of your personal data.</li><li _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="">Please be aware that, although we endeavour to provide reasonable security for information we process and maintain, no security system can prevent all potential security breaches.</li></ol></li><li _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166=""><h2 _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="">CHANGES</h2><p _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="" class="d-block">We will notify you of any changes to this policy by email, notice on the website and/or account message.</p></li><li _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166=""><h2 _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="">INTERNATIONAL DATA TRANSFERS</h2><p _ngcontent-eyeora-vr-v2-c166="">Where we transfer your data outside of the EEA in respect of the transfer to the above affiliates, we have agreements in place with those parties which include standard data protection clauses adopted by a data protection regulator and approved by the European Commission to ensure that appropriate safeguards are in place to protect your Personal Data.
